    LEFT JOIN "ProductImage" AS p8 ON p5."ProductVariantId" = p8."ProductVariantId"
) AS s0 ON p."ProductId" = s0."ProductId"
WHERE p."ProductApprovalStatusId" = 4 AND p."ProductStatusId" = 2 AND EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM "ProductVariant" AS p0
    WHERE p."ProductId" = p0."ProductId" AND p0."ProductApprovalStatusId" = 4 AND p0."ProductVariantStatusId" = 2 AND EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM "Inventory" AS i
        WHERE p0."ProductVariantId" = i."ProductVariantId" AND i."AvailableQuantity" > 0))
ORDER BY p."ProductId", p1."ProductApprovalStatusId", p2."ProductStatusId", p3."ProductSubCategoryId", v."VendorId", p4."ProductImageId", s0."ProductVariantId", s0."InventoryId", s0."ProductVariantAttributeId", s0."ProductSubCategoryAttributeId0", s0."AttributeMasterId0"

INNER JOIN "ProductVariant" AS p ON c."ProductVariantId" = p."ProductVariantId"
INNER JOIN "Product" AS p0 ON p."ProductId" = p0."ProductId"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i."InventoryId", i."AddressId", i."AvailableQuantity", i."IsActive", i."ProductVariantId", i."ReservedQuantity", i."UpdatedAt", a."AddressId" AS "AddressId0", a."AddressLine", a."City", a."ContactName", a."ContactPhoneNumber", a."Country", a."CreatedAt", a."IsDefault", a."LandMark", a."PinCode", a."State", a."UpdatedAt" AS "UpdatedAt0", a."UserId"
    FROM "Inventory" AS i
    INNER JOIN "Address" AS a ON i."AddressId" = a."AddressId"
) AS s ON p."ProductVariantId" = s."ProductVariantId"
WHERE c0."UserId" = @userId
ORDER BY c."CartItemsId", c0."CartId", p."ProductVariantId", p0."ProductId", s."InventoryId"
